|Defining Criteria=anatomy
|Definition=The limbic lobe is a synthetic lobe located on the medial margin (or limbus) of the hemisphere.<br>Composed of adjacent portions of the frontal, parietal, and temporal lobes that surround the corpus callosum, the limbic lobe is involved with autonomic and related somatic behavioral activities.<br/>The limbic lobe receives input from thalamic nuclei that are connected with parts of the hypothalamus and with the hippocampal formation, a primitive cortical structure within the inferior horn of the lateral ventricle.

'''tract_(Homo sapiens)'''
{{Connectome Brain Region
|Abbreviation=tract
|Species=Homo sapiens
|English Name=Tract
|Latin Name=
|Other Name=
|Defining Criteria=
|Definition=Tracts are defined here as a set of brain regions (starts and terminations of the tracts) as well as a set of brain connections, usually connecting the brain regions. Often, the tract relates to a sensory or motor system. The particular details, like the functional ordering of the stations, have to be described on the individual tract pages, since this wiki does not yet implement functional parthood relationships.
|Function Tag=
}}
